During the stay, the service staff often actively serve you, such as calling you in advance to ask if you have any specific requirements for the room, providing you with luggage check-in, asking you what drinks you need at breakfast, and actively asking if you have any dining needs, etc. These thoughtful services make you feel at home.
Let's talk about the details of the hotel. After checking in, we were immediately told that we were upgraded to the executive room on the top floor, and we also enjoyed the executive lounge service, which made people feel very happy. In the buffet breakfast, the hotel is also not vague. During the Spring Festival, when the passenger flow is relatively large, the hotel's hot milk has never been out of stock. If there is residue in the hotel's food area, the waiter will clean it immediately.
Let's talk about the hotel's hardware. The top floor can overlook the entire Pinghu Lake, and the executive lounge can overlook the full view of Jiulong Mountain. The internal facilities also have capsule coffee machines, yoga mats, dumbbells, Bluetooth speakers and other equipment, allowing people to enjoy the pleasure of travel without leaving home.
One drawback is that the hotel provides too little toothpaste, which is basically used up after one use. Although I understand that the hotel is doing this for environmental protection, it still needs to consider the actual situation of the residents.
